msg:A very well run service apartment located within the Olympic Youth Centre in the Hexi District. The location is not central but in a fairly new-ish developing district. The apartment itself is very well maintained, clean and the ayis (cleaning staff) are very detailed oriented. Room size is spacious and all apartment facilities are provided including a dishwasher, washing machine, etc. Food wise, there are plenty of choices across the road in the form of Japanese and Singaporean cuisine. The Singaporean one, though, was a bit off the expected Singaporean taste. It passes for locals but not for those who have sampled true Singaporean flavours. The Olympic Youth Centre can get rather busy if a conference is taking place. Avoid taking the breakfast on the 2nd floor if it is very busy and have it on the 43rd floor.

info:Classic Apartment
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:34 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:Service: Xiaolan at the front desk had a good service attitude and explained the precautions for going up and down the elevator clearly. The service attitude of the housekeeping staff who came to deliver things was also good.
The room size and hotel facilities are not mentioned. By the way, there is free afternoon tea in the lobby in the afternoon.
The details of the room need to be improved:
1. The trash can is relatively old, at least the trash can in room 5110 is relatively old. You can consider a trash can that can match the room type better but is more durable.
2. The light buttons in the toilet have blurred printing on some buttons due to long-term touch. You can consider pasting labels, but make the labels more wear-resistant, or update the printing regularly.
3. The floor beside the bed has a noticeable sense of collapse when you step on it, at least in room 5110. It is recommended to repair it.
4. Although the toilet washbasin is Kohler, the water core is not tight enough. If it takes a long time, it is recommended to replace it with a press-type water core.
5. The toilet seat cushion, although the toilet is also Kohler, it feels very cold when you sit on it suddenly. When you need to replace or repair it after a long time, you can consider the material of the cushion.
Overall, I recommend staying here.
